Style Change Notification\\nFile: layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp — RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent\\n\\nWhen a CSS property is mutated (e.g., via JS element.style.color='red' or a class change), RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent() is called with the affected Element, a RestyleHint, and optionally an nsChangeHint. This calls Servo_NoteExplicitHints() (a Rust FFI call into the Servo style engine) to mark the element as needing restyling, and sets the 'restyle root' on the document for the next style flush.\\n\\n## 2. Style Traversal and Frame Style Recomputation\\nFiles: layout/style/ServoStyleSet.cpp, layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp\\nSymbols: ServoStyleSet::StyleDocument, RestyleManager::DoProcessPendingRestyles, RestyleManager::ProcessPostTraversal\\n\\nDuring the next style flush (PresShell::DoFlushPendingNotifications calls mPresContext->RestyleManager()->ProcessPendingRestyles()), DoProcessPendingRestyles() calls ServoStyleSet::StyleDocument() which invokes Servo_TraverseSubtree() — the parallel Servo style traversal that recomputes ComputedStyle for all dirty elements. After traversal, RestyleManager::ProcessPostTraversal() is called on each restyled element. It calls Servo_TakeChangeHint() to retrieve the computed nsChangeHint for the element's frame and appends it to an nsStyleChangeList.\\n\\n## 3. Dirty-Frame Reflow Scheduling\\nFiles: layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp, layout/base/PresShell.cpp\\nSymbols: RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames, StyleChangeReflow (static), PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow\\n\\nRestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames() iterates over the nsStyleChangeList and processes each change hint. For reflow-requiring hints (nsChangeHint_NeedReflow, nsChangeHint_ClearAncestorIntrinsics, etc.), the static function StyleChangeReflow() is called. StyleChangeReflow() determines the IntrinsicDirty type and dirty bits, then calls PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow() on the affected frame(s). FrameNeedsReflow marks the frame and ancestors with NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY / NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN bits and adds the frame to mDirtyRoots (the reflow queue). For paint-only hints (nsChangeHint_RepaintFrame), frame->SchedulePaint() is called directly.\\n\\n## 4. Reflow Execution\\nFile: layout/base/PresShell.cpp\\nSymbols: PresShell::DoFlushLayout, PresShell::ProcessReflowCommands\\n\\nPresShell::DoFlushLayout() (called from DoFlushPendingNotifications when flushType >= FlushType::Layout) calls ProcessReflowCommands(). This iterates mDirtyRoots, popping the shallowest dirty root and calling DoReflow() on it to perform full box model layout for the dirty subtree, updating frame sizes and positions.\\n\\n## 5. Display List Construction\\nFiles: layout/base/nsLayoutUtils.cpp, layout/painting/nsDisplayList.cpp\\nSymbols: nsLayoutUtils::PaintFrame, nsDisplayList::PaintRoot\\n\\nWhen the widget needs to repaint (driven by the refresh driver), nsLayoutUtils::PaintFrame() is called. It creates an nsDisplayListBuilder and calls aFrame->BuildDisplayListForStackingContext() on the root frame, which recursively dispatches BuildDisplayList() on every frame in the tree. This constructs a flat nsDisplayList of typed display items (backgrounds, borders, text, transforms, opacity layers, etc.). The builder also handles retained display lists for partial updates (RetainedDisplayListBuilder::AttemptPartialUpdate). The completed list is passed to nsDisplayList::PaintRoot().\\n\\n## 6. WebRender Layer Update\\nFiles: layout/painting/nsDisplayList.cpp, gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderLayerManager.cpp, gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderCommandBuilder.cpp, gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderBridgeParent.cpp, gfx/webrender_bindings/WebRenderAPI.cpp\\nSymbols: WebRenderLayerManager::EndTransactionWithoutLayer, WebRenderCommandBuilder::BuildWebRenderCommands, WebRenderCommandBuilder::CreateWebRenderCommandsFromDisplayList, WebRenderBridgeParent::RecvSetDisplayList\\n\\nnsDisplayList::PaintRoot() detects the WebRender backend (renderer->GetBackendType() == LayersBackend::LAYERS_WR) and calls WebRenderLayerManager::EndTransactionWithoutLayer(). This begins a WebRender transaction (WrBridge()->BeginTransaction()), creates a wr::DisplayListBuilder, and calls WebRenderCommandBuilder::BuildWebRenderCommands() which in turn calls CreateWebRenderCommandsFromDisplayList(). This function walks the Gecko nsDisplayList and emits corresponding WebRender display list primitives (rects, images, text glyphs, stacking contexts, clip chains, scroll layers) into the wr::DisplayListBuilder. The builder is finalized with DisplayListBuilder::End() serializing it to a byte buffer. WrBridge()->EndTransaction() sends the DisplayListData over IPC to the compositor process, where WebRenderBridgeParent::RecvSetDisplayList() / ProcessDisplayListData() forwards it to the WebRender scene builder thread. WebRender then rebuilds the scene (applies the new display list) and schedules a composite frame.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
